Northwest of Harbin: Railway Tracks Destroyed Again; Fierce Battle Near Sartu All Night 55

(Harbin) Near Sartu (transliteration) on the Chinese Eastern Railway, about ninety miles northwest of Harbin, bandits once again dismantled the tracks yesterday, attempting to rob the Siberian express train. The bandits numbered about four hundred, and had already removed the spikes from a section of the track. The commander of the Anda area defense of the Chinese Eastern Railway received advance notice and immediately dispatched Japanese infantry, cavalry, and artillery to Sartu, where they encountered the bandits. A fierce battle ensued all night, and the bandits were unable to withstand the attack and retreated, suffering heavy casualties. This morning, the express train passed over the track without spikes, but fortunately, no accident occurred. (19th, Reuters)

Kwantung Army of Japan and South Manchuria Railway Reorganization Plan; Military Headquarters Fully Supports; Determined to Overcome All Difficulties and Negotiate with the Government; Will Cause Significant Political Waves 56

(Tokyo) Regarding the reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway (SMR), Hirai, the Army Paymaster who was on a business trip to Manchuria, returned to Tokyo last night on the special express "Fuji." He immediately went to the Army Ministry to submit the reorganization plan to Yamaoka, the Director of the Military Affairs Bureau. Before entering Tokyo, Paymaster Hirai told reporters in the train that although the contents of the SMR reorganization plan could absolutely not be disclosed, he was confident that there was absolutely no shortage of funds and that the limit for expanding the issuance of corporate bonds was sufficient, so there was no need to worry. Even if the Ministry of Colonial Affairs opposes it, we have a full chance of winning. (19th, Communication Society)

(Tokyo) The Army Ministry received a detailed report from Paymaster Hirai regarding the SMR reorganization last night and decided to start the review from today. After consulting with the General Staff Headquarters, the Army's attitude will be determined when the work is completed, and then consultations will be held with the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, and other relevant authorities. As for the general outline, it is determined to overcome all difficulties and implement the original plan. (19th, Communication Society)

(Tokyo) After Lin and Hatta, the President and Vice President of the SMR, arrived in Tokyo, the SMR reorganization plan was handed over to the central government. The Ministry of Finance, in view of the importance of this case, has independently studied the problem and plans to submit the Ministry of Finance's SMR reorganization plan when necessary and make concrete preparations. The Ministry of Finance's attitude is to absolutely oppose the so-called fundamental policy of the Kwantung Army to control the supervision of the SMR. It also holds the opinion that the SMR's development of Manchurian resources must be supplied with a large amount of capital from mainland Japan. The Ministry of Finance has the right to supervise the raising of funds in the central government, so it considers the financial market situation in mainland Japan and guides the SMR, so that the "State of Manchuria" can develop healthily. Reorganizing the SMR into an ordinary holding company would merely be a management company, losing the interest of the enterprise and preventing capital from entering "Manchuria." (19th, Japanese Alliance)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Colonial Affairs not only strongly opposes the SMR reorganization plan, but also the government leaders such as Prime Minister Saito, Finance Minister Takahashi, and Home Minister Yamamoto all oppose it. Publicly appointed members of the House of Peers, such as the Koseikai, also have dissenting opinions. The Seiyukai and Minseito parties in the House of Representatives have not explicitly criticized it due to the influence of the military, but generally oppose it. The reasons for the opposition from various aspects are: 1. According to the on-site plan, the SMR will be disintegrated and become a holding company. This is what happens when companies are merged into one company. If this one company is separated this time, it will lose its essence. 2. The so-called holding company has supervisory power over the companies under its control. If the plan is approved this time, the supervisory power will be in the hands of the military, and the holding company will become a simple securities company, resulting in instability. 3. Investors will be hesitant to invest in such an unstable company. Also, it must be said that it is a mistake for the military to have supervisory power. 4. Among the separated companies, railways and coal mines can be operated independently, but glass, ammonium sulfate, and other affiliated companies cannot be independent. With the current organization, overall benefits can be obtained, etc. Therefore, the future situation will become a considerable political problem. (19th, Telecommunication)

Interest on Due Foreign Debt: Germany Announces Reduced Payment; Dawes and Young Loans to be Paid as Scheduled; London Expresses Dissatisfaction and Prepares to Protest 57

(Berlin) Dr. Schacht, President of the Deutsche Bank, stated in the central committee of the bank today that Germany will only pay 30% of the interest due on long-term foreign debt in cash in the next six months, instead of the 50% paid in the past six months. The remaining 70% will be paid with Deutsche Bank Mark certificates. Subsequently, the bank issued a public statement explaining the necessity of reducing cash payments, stating that although trade has recently been in surplus, the value of exports is not entirely paid in foreign currency, but is paid with Deutsche Bank Mark certificates and German debt instruments, resulting in insufficient foreign currency to pay the large amount of interest due. However, the Dawes and Young loans are not subject to this rule, and the repayment of private debts will also be regulated separately. (18th, National Press)

(London) British government officials and financial leaders have publicly expressed dissatisfaction today with Germany's reduction of cash payments for interest on foreign debts, and the situation is quite serious. It is expected that protests will be lodged with Berlin through diplomatic channels. The British government has begun to contact British bankers and representatives of German creditors in order to determine what action to take. It is understood that British Ambassador to Germany, Sir Eric Phipps, will convey the British government's protest to the German government upon his return to Berlin. Sir Eric attended a meeting of the British Cabinet Disarmament Committee today and was ordered to convey Britain's recent disarmament proposals to German Chancellor Hitler. (19th, National Press)

(London) Today's newspapers severely criticized France's incomplete fulfillment of its debt obligations, stating that Germany's difficulties are undeniable. Germany tried its best to maintain its credit in July, but that is not the case now. It wants to pay debts denominated in foreign currency with new Marks and use the unpaid balance to promote German exports. This principle is very dangerous. Germany used to have a reputation as an honest debtor, but now its reputation has been ruined. Furthermore, it pays all debts to Switzerland and the Netherlands due to their import concessions, and this kind of discriminatory treatment is especially unacceptable. Since June 30, the German National Bank's reserves have increased from 13 million pounds to 20 million pounds, and at the same time, Germany's monthly trade balance has gradually improved. This fact should give people hope that interest will increase and debts will not be defaulted. Germans replied that the average monthly trade balance is only 60 million Marks, while the amount to be paid is more than 100 million Marks. Brokers at the London Stock Exchange have asked their board to prohibit German municipal authorities that do not fulfill their debt obligations from buying low-value German government bonds on the London market. (19th, Reuters)

US Treasury Secretary Satisfied with Gold Purchase Results; Prices Increase by 5.5 Percent 58

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau responded today to the statement issued by Brooklyn College that the authorities' gold purchase policy cannot be relied upon to restore prices, but instead hinders recovery, saying that the government's gold purchase program has increased prices by 5.5 percent, which he considers satisfactory. He also said that the Treasury Department bought 1.6 million yuan worth of government bonds last week, and since October 21, the price of gold has increased by 16 percent and prices have increased by 5.5 percent. (18th, Reuters) (Chicago) Professor Allen, a well-known Chicago economist, claimed that although industry and commerce have made some progress in the past year, they are still 35 to 40 percent lower than usual. The price of ordinary industrial shares, calculated in devalued gold yuan, has risen by 65 percent, but calculated in gold coins, it has only risen by 6 percent, so it is still 35 percent lower than in 1926. In his opinion, given the weakness of world prices, there is no room for optimism. The prospects for 1934 largely depend on whether the US President's plan is sound and has healing power. It is wise for the US President to refuse to reset the price of the gold yuan at this time. (18th, National Press)

French Finance Minister Announces Opposition to Inflation; Will Raise 20 Billion Francs in Debt 59

(Paris) French Finance Minister Bonnet declared during a Senate debate on the finance bill today, "We will oppose inflation and will not change." (19th, Reuters)

(Paris) It is now generally understood that the French government must soon raise 20 billion francs in debt to meet its 1934 debt obligations. However, the success of this debt depends on the balance of the budget. The finance bill is currently being debated in the parliament, but it will pass anyway. The Senate has decided to debate the bill for three days, and today is the second day. It is expected that it will be approved at the end of this week in the same wording as the House of Representatives has already passed. Although the rapporteur mentioned the emptiness of the treasury, the reappearance of floating debt, and the increase in public debt, Finance Minister Bonnet declared today that the situation is not as dangerous as it is rumored. The government is determined to restore national finances and avoid inflation. Regarding the debt-raising proposal, it is worth noting that the banknotes and cash stored by the French people are worth about 30 billion francs. (19th, Reuters)

Japanese Political Parties Seek Cooperation to Resist Military Interference in Politics; Uphold the Ruling Power of Financial Groups; Oppose Fascist Revolution; Another Member of the Seiyukai Party Defects 60

Claims to be willing to sacrifice himself to protect the party's reputation

(Tokyo) Various Japanese fascist groups deeply resent the Saito cabinet as a puppet of the financial groups and have been holding meetings for days to overthrow the cabinet and promote fascist dictatorship. They are vigorously inciting the poor to riot at the end of the year and have decided to gather farmers from various places in the name of petitioning during the National Assembly meeting in January, surround the National Assembly, and implement a fascist revolution. Among the members of the National League, there is no shortage of those who respond to this group. The Seiyukai and Minseito parties are very worried, and their leaders are secretly traveling frequently to discuss ways to cooperate and deal with the situation. It has been decided to determine the time for a joint celebration of the leaders of the two parties and the method of cooperation in one or two months. For the sake of upholding the ruling power of the financial groups, the two parties have decided to clean up military discipline and oppose military interference in politics as an important political program for their cooperation. (19th, China United Press) (Tokyo) Shiotsuki Gaku, a Seiyukai member elected from Oita Prefecture, who was implicated in the Tokyo City Scandal and was accused in the case, announced his defection from the Seiyukai today. He also stated that the reputation of Japanese political parties has fallen to the ground. He himself is now suspected by the world because of his implication in the Tokyo City Scandal, so he will preemptively defect from the political party to thank the people of the country before the court makes a judgment on right and wrong. This move is believed to be able to restore the people's trust in political parties. There are still eleven people in the Seiyukai, including former Railways Minister Ogawa, Nakajima, Suzuki, and Idoi, who are implicated in the embezzlement case. Shiotsuki's defection has given them an important hint and has attracted attention from all walks of life. (11th, China United Press)

Japanese Cabinet Meeting: Ministers Engage in Heated Debate; Difficult to Implement Rural Policies 61

(Tokyo) At 1:30 PM today, the Japanese cabinet convened an internal affairs meeting. Prime Minister Saito originally planned to conclude today, but due to the many disputes, nothing was gained. The ministers' views on the principles of saving agriculture are not far apart, but their specific proposals differ too much. Agriculture Minister Goto raised the issue of rural joint organizations, fertilizer countermeasures, rural land rights, protection of tenant farmers, and additional budgets. Regarding the rural joint organization plan, Commerce Minister Nakajima, representing the views of the financial groups, opposed expanding industrial organizations and eliminating small and medium-sized businesses and industries. Fertilizer countermeasures will be handled by the agricultural and commercial authorities to formulate specific measures. Because the land issue harms the interests of the landlord class, the two ministers, Mitsuchi and Takahashi, strongly opposed it, and the budget issue was not raised. It is reported that Army Minister Araki raised a major incident in Manchuria in the meeting and reported the truth of the matter. Regarding the SMR reorganization plan, Army Minister Araki also criticized Colonial Affairs Minister Nagai in person. Colonial Affairs Minister Nagai said that he did not make a statement, but that his conversation was mistakenly reported as a statement. The heated debate lasted for three and a half hours before the meeting adjourned. It is expected that it will be difficult to conclude by the end of the year. (19th, China United Press)

Ministry of Interior: Water Conservancy Conference Opens; Huang Shaoxiong Delivers Opening Remarks; Approximately Twenty Proposals 66

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior's Water Conservancy Conference opened on the morning of the 19th. The following 27 people attended: Li Shutian, Sun Fushi, Zhang Raoying, Teng Gu, Zhu Shijun, Chen Maojie, Huang Qianyi, Xu Shida, Zhou Xiangxian, Song Xishang, Zheng Zhenyu, Wang Hucheng, Xu Xinwu, Huang Bizhi, Chen Ganen, Yang Baopu, Sun Turui, Mei Ru'ao, Liu Yinbi, Xu Tinghu, Shen Baixian, Gao Bingfang, Xu Kai, Lin Pingyi, Shen Baojun, Mao Yisheng, and Hu Pinyuan. Chairman Huang Shaoxiong delivered the opening remarks. Li Shutian and Zhou Xiangxian described the importance of water conservancy in our country. It is reported that in addition to discussing the draft Water Law and hydrological measurement, etc., the representatives proposed about twenty proposals: 1. Scope of water conservancy, 2. Water administration system, 3. Water Conservancy Advisory Council, 4. Procedures for water demand, 5. Revocation of water conservancy, 6. Types of water rights registration, 7. Scope of water rights exempted from registration, 8. Restrictions on flood discharge, 9. Water storage and drainage, 10. Water conservancy funds, 11. Land acquisition, 12. Penalties, which must be discussed separately. The conference was originally scheduled for the 19th and 20th, but due to the large number of proposals, it was extended by one day. (19th, Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The internal affairs department held an opening ceremony for the water conservancy conference at 9:00 AM on the 19th. More than 30 people from various water conservancy agencies and experts attended. Chairman Huang Shaoxiong presided over the meeting, and Teng Gu was dispatched by the Executive Yuan to attend. After Huang Shaoxiong gave the opening remarks, Teng Gu and the representatives gave speeches one after another. Then, the water law was discussed. In the afternoon, a group photo was taken to commemorate the event. (19th, Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Song Xishang said that more than 70 breaches of the Yellow River had been blocked one after another, but the breach at Shitou Village was difficult to block. The breach required approximately 1 million yuan and 8,000 cubic meters of stone. He asked the Ministry of Railways to transport the stone free of charge and hire ferry craftsmen to drive piles. It could be completed by next spring. Song will return to Kaifeng on the 23rd. (19th, Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Li Shutian said that although there are many hydrological records of rivers in North China, they are still insufficient for reference and must be continuously surveyed. Currently, there are about 20 hydrological stations, about 40 water level stations, and about 80 rain gauge stations, distributed in the Jinan, Kaifeng, Taiyuan, and Chengde areas. The fundamental plan for the governance of the Yongding River is to divert the turbid current to Beihai and dredge Qinglong Bay, which will cost approximately 34 million yuan. If the Yongding River is not governed, the silt in the Hai River will not be removed, and the port of Tianjin will not be improved. The most important project now requires approximately 5 million yuan, which has been submitted by the Water Conservancy Association to the central government for allocation from cotton and wheat loans for implementation. (19th, Special Dispatch)

Hebei and Henan Representatives Arrive in Jinan to Attend the Yellow River Conference; Proposals from Hebei and Henan Provinces 67

(Jinan) Chen Ruzhen, Director of the Henan River Bureau, Feng Chunxi, Representative of the Hebei River Bureau, and Zhu Mingzhuo, Representative of the Henan Provincial Government, all arrived in Jinan today to attend the Three-Province River Bureau Conference on the 20th. Feng said that the blocking of the breach at Shitou Village could be completed this winter, but the construction was difficult due to lack of funds. Formal construction had not yet begun. Permeable dams and water diversion dams were being built, and the 500,000 yuan construction fund might not be enough. Only 170,000 yuan had been allocated, and only 1,000 cubic meters of stone had been transported. He brought five proposals: 1. The Taihang Dam at the border of Hebei and Henan should be repaired by the government, 2. The Lao'an Dam in Hua County should be repaired by the government, 3. Add river police, 4. Raise the dikes, 5. Add water volume reports to the hydrological station in Shaanzhou. The riverbed of the Dacheji River in Changyuan is higher than the river dike and the dike is being raised. (19th, Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Chen Ruzhen said that the Henan breach blocking project could be completed within three days. However, all of the Yellow River water from the name of the village has flowed from the breach, and cars can now pass through the old riverbed. The conference will open on the 20th to review the proposals. On the 21st, five proposals from Henan will be discussed: 1. Establish material factories along the river, 2. Ask the Yellow River Conservancy Commission to release silt along the river to prevent flooding and benefit the people's livelihood, 3. Ask the Commission to set up a hydraulic experiment field along the river, 4. Ask the Commission to measure the Yellow River downstream of Henan Province, 5. Continue to determine the border area between Hebei, Pingyuan, and Henan for river defense to facilitate river defense. In addition, Hebei, Shandong, and Henan will jointly ask the governments of Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, and Anhui to forward a request to the central government to allocate a large sum of money to repair the Yellow River post-disaster project to prevent breaches next year, because next year will be more dangerous than this year. (19th, Special Dispatch)

Wang Chonghui's International Missions 83

(Nanjing) According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the international judicial institutions in The Hague originally included two types: the Permanent Court of Arbitration and the Permanent Court of International Justice. The former is based on the Hague Convention of 1899 and 1907, while the latter is based on the Statute of the Permanent Court of International Justice, unanimously adopted by the League of Nations General Assembly on December 13, 1920. Wang Chonghui has served as the Chinese arbitrator of the Court of Arbitration since 1921, and was elected as a judge of the Permanent Court of International Justice after September 1930, assuming office in April 1931. These are two separate matters. Recently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a report from the Chinese envoy stationed in the Netherlands stating that Wang's term as arbitrator expired on November 26 of last year and can be renewed according to Article 44 of the Second Hague Convention. This was forwarded to the Executive Yuan for reappointment. As for Wang's position as a judge of the Permanent Court of International Justice, his term should be nine years according to Article 13 of the Statute of the Permanent Court of International Justice. Wang only went to The Hague two years ago. The reports in various newspapers have confused the Court of Arbitration in The Hague with the Permanent Court of International Justice in The Hague, leading to misunderstandings. (19th Special Telegram)

Trotsky of Russia Discusses Japan's Impending Suicide 丨Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Entrusts Matsuoka to Write a Rebuttal丨 103

On the 14th of this month, the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun reprinted an article from the famous American magazine "Records" in which Russian Trotsky vehemently attacked Japan. Entitled "Is Japan Really Committing Suicide?" The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs entrusted Yosuke Matsuoka to write a rebuttal. The following is a summary of the main points of Trotsky and Madame Drummond-Hay's views on the Russo-Japanese War.

Madame Drummond-Hay recently published an article in the Hearst News Service in the United States, titled "Views on the Russo-Japanese War," predicting that Japan will inevitably fight Russia and the United States. This kind of rumor is also heard among Russians, who fear that Japan's emerging power will extend its strategic hand into Russia. Russia will inevitably lose its gateway to the Far East, Vladivostok, and the coastal region. Trotsky, on the other hand, said that after the World War, a great tragedy in human history is about to occur in Japan. The Japanese often boast of never losing a war. People believe that this belief has little to do with Japan's economy and society, but they do not know that Japan's ruling class is even more powerful than before. Therefore, the internal trends of these people have all turned to aggressive foreign issues. Regarding the recent request to Russia to recognize "Manchukuo," they regard international treaties as waste paper and ignore the investigation by the League of Nations. On the one hand, they hope that the United States will adhere to a policy of non-interference, and on the other hand, they want Russia to make major concessions, allowing Japan to act freely. As a result, Japan not only has ambitions to dominate Asia, but even wants to dominate the entire world. This is a fantasy held by the Japanese. However, the occurrence of this fantasy, observed from past facts, is like the Japanese defeating China in a war forty years ago, and driving Russia out of Manchuria thirty years ago. These are past facts, but in today's terms, they are already process fantasies. Therefore, modern Japan's desire to defeat Russia or other first-class countries may not be easy. First, a long-term war requires a calculation of success in economic warfare. Today's Japanese military personnel cannot be compared with the United States and Russia in terms of modern scientific knowledge. The final decision of Japan's great invasion is made by the military leaders, but are they miscalculating the war plans of the world's number one land power? The Japanese boast of never losing a war because they over-believe in the myths of past victories, or only compare themselves with countries that are lagging behind the times. The relative evaluation of victory depends entirely on the facts. Moreover, those who defeated Russia in the past cannot be compared with today. Seven years after the Russo-Japanese War, the Russian army has been greatly reformed, and Japan often assumes that Russia and the United States are hypothetical enemy countries. However, Japan's economy is weak, and its domestic factories want to continue the war for several years, and its ability to supply the necessary supplies to the battlefield is very weak. Other economic organizations are heavily burdened by the military in peacetime, and they also lack experience in modern science and modern tactics. Madame Drummond-Hay commented, "Today, Russia's only method of attacking Japan is the air force. The distance between the coastal region and Japan is only 350 nautical miles, and the maximum distance is no more than 750 nautical miles. If Vladivostok is equipped with long-range aircraft with four motors to attack Japan, it can achieve the purpose of attack, but the air force cannot completely return. Because Japan has fully defended against the development of the Chinese and Russian air forces, Japan's aviation is still in its infancy. At present, Russia's air force expansion is mainly based on building and equipping four to five large bombers, while Japan specializes in building aircraft, artillery, and fighter jets that are mainly defensive. What will be the result if a war breaks out between Japan and Russia? From a strategic point of view, Japan is not necessarily at a disadvantage. Because Japan's air force has an advantage over the Russian air force, that is, its defense area is small, and aircraft manufacturing plants are all close to the base. Russia does not have complete manufacturing and repair factories near the base. For example, if Vladivostok is attacked by the Japanese air force, or the Siberian railway is blocked, it will not be easy to organize. A few days ago, Russia announced its air force expansion plan. Many people did not believe it, but in today's world, it cannot be disbelieved. Fifteen years ago, when the European War broke out, Germany had only 280 aircraft. By 1918, when the armistice treaty was signed, there were 5,000 aircraft on the front line, 9,000 aircraft in the rear, and 5,500 aircraft unfinished in the factory. Moreover, with the development of modern aviation industry, Russia's expansion of the air force should not be underestimated."

Shantou's Financial Circles Still in Panic 104

The Appeasement Headquarters Issues a Proclamation to Maintain Paper Money

The Market's Current Funds Are Extremely Exhausted

Shantou Correspondence: Shantou's various private banks issued approximately 3 million yuan in paper money, of which approximately 1 million yuan has already collapsed. In addition, 58 private banks issued blank notes, totaling 1.55 million yuan. Currently, five banks have collapsed, with a total of 219,000 yuan in blank notes. The City Chamber of Commerce, in response to the collapse of various private banks and the people's years of hardship, telegraphed the Provincial Government, requesting a temporary suspension of the collection of various taxes, and submitted a report to the Eastern District Appeasement Headquarters, requesting relief. The Headquarters has now issued a proclamation to the people, stating that from now on, they must not refuse to use the collapsed paper money and blank notes. The original text is as follows: "Yesterday, Chairman Zheng Lingxing of the City Chamber of Commerce reported that Guangfa, Zhifa, Hongfasheng, Qianchangxing and other private banks simultaneously declared bankruptcy today, and a major panic suddenly arose in the city's financial circles. In order to maintain the market, the Association immediately convened an emergency executive committee meeting, which resolved three measures regarding maintaining the market's finances: 1. The guaranteed paper money and guaranteed blank notes issued by various firms and banks throughout the city are, in fact, secured by industry and can fundamentally be worry-free. They should all be used as usual to maintain the market. From today onwards, it is resolved not to redeem them within these four months. 2. Regardless of what kind of bank or private bank, those with due dates for withdrawal from today onwards will all have their bills extended for 60 days, with a daily interest rate of 2.5 cents per thousand yuan for private banks and 3 cents for other banks. This is to maintain the overall situation in the city. If there is intentional collection and return, it will be regarded as damaging finance. In addition to requesting official punishment, each household will also be fined 500 yuan in silver dollars. 3. For deposits made by wealthy households, whether they are in banks or private banks, if they want to withdraw them, from today onwards, they will only be allowed to withdraw 10% of the amount deposited each month. Transactions between private banks and banks will still be carried out as usual. Regarding Guangfa, Zhifa, Hongfasheng, etc., the resolutions for the guaranteed blank notes and guaranteed paper money are as follows: Guangfa Bank issued 110,000 yuan in guaranteed paper money and 50,000 yuan in guaranteed blank notes; Zhifa Bank issued 100,000 yuan in guaranteed paper money and 36,500 yuan in guaranteed blank notes; Hongfasheng Bank issued 50,000 yuan in guaranteed paper money. All of these are secured by local industries and can fundamentally be worry-free. However, once this huge amount of money stagnates, it will have a significant impact on the market. It is agreed that the Association will be responsible for stamping the paper money and blank notes issued by the above three banks with the City of Shantou Chamber of Commerce circulation stamp. During these four months, they will be used as usual and must not be rejected. Violators will be investigated by the authorities. The above two items are all measures to maintain the market's finances and should be reported to the authorities for record and announced to the public. In addition to submitting a separate report, a list of the Guangfa Bank's etc. guaranteed industries is attached for your review. Upon investigation, the various items presented by the Chairman are for the purpose of maintaining the market's finances and are, of course, feasible. Since the Guangfa Bank's etc. guaranteed paper money and blank notes are secured by local industries, the public can be worry-free. In addition to instructing that this matter be recorded, it is hereby proclaimed to merchants and residents for their information."

Currently, Shantou's established private banks are all strictly controlling lending. The Bank of China, the Postal Bureau, and other institutions have suspended receiving deposits and savings, because the majority of the money received consists of paper money and blank notes. The various tax bureaus all require the collection of silver dollars and cash. Established wealthy families are secretly buying Hong Kong dollars for storage, so the price of Hong Kong dollars is particularly high, with a premium of 230 yuan per thousand yuan. Shanghai drafts are also high, with a premium of 89 yuan per hundred yuan. This is a sign that the people are unwilling to hold paper money. With the exchange rate so high, there are more and more people smuggling cash out of the country. The exhaustion of cash in the market is unprecedented since Shantou was established. (13th)

The People of Northern Sichuan Are Forming Volunteer Corps 105

Hardships Suffered by the People of Yingshan Disrupted by Banditry, as Described by Refugees

Peng'an Correspondence: Whenever the Red Bandits arrive at a place, they completely concentrate all the grain and cash in that place, and order the people of that place to organize various teams to serve them. Women with even a little beauty are almost all raped by the bandits, and are forced to organize comfort teams for the bandit army to insult at will. Therefore, the people all resent them to the bone. In recent days, the five-route bandit suppression army has been fiercely attacking the bandits who claimed allegiance to the Soviets, inflicting heavy losses on the bandits. Therefore, the people in various places have risen up and organized volunteer corps to jointly assist the government army in suppressing the bandits. It is estimated that those that have been organized and established include various counties such as Shunqing, Peng'an, Yingshan, Yilong, Nanbu, and Quxian. Even the people of Tongnanba, who have fallen into the bandit area, have all risen up upon hearing the news. These teams are extremely good at fighting, and they know the tactics of the Red Bandits very well. Recently, they sent people to contact Yang Sen and Li Qixiang to request assistance and have established contact. There are also many defectors from the bandit army, and the momentum is very large. The Red Bandits, seeing this situation, are very panicked, and the people's hearts are shaking. The situation is extremely chaotic. Although Yingshan has now been recovered, it was destroyed and is beyond repair after being captured by the bandits. Recently, someone escaped here and described the situation in Yingshan as follows:

After Yingshan City was captured by the communist bandits, He Wei, the commander of the pseudo-Ninth Army, was stationed there and set up a Likin Tax Committee. The opium and pork tax was 30%, and there was no fixed tax amount for other products. The people were ordered to make a pair of shoes for each household. Those who could not make them had to buy a pair of thread-eared straw sandals as comfort items for the officers and soldiers of the pseudo-army. Local people who were identified as wealthy were immediately taken to the political department for punishment and forced to hand over their money. Those who could not hand over the money were executed. When the bandits retreated, they detained more than 500 men, women, old and young. Many died along the way, and the rest were detained in the political department.

After the communist bandits came to the city, no one who had not escaped was tied up. The bandits searched for grain and rice in the residents' homes, taking whatever they could eat or wear. The people could only cry to the heavens and pray to the gods. When we (the gentleman referred to himself) went out to walk, we had to get a road pass. If two or three people were chatting together, they would say that they were reactionaries and arbitrarily arrest and whip them. Families were not allowed to gather in one place. At 6:00 PM in the evening, the lights had to be turned off. If it was a little late, they would say that there was trackless behavior. If there were missing slogans on the street, they would say that we tore them down, restricting freedom more than being a slave of a vanquished country.

The bandits set up five villages in the city, one each in the southwest, northeast, and one in the People's Bookstore opposite the county government, with 150 households in each village. Each village had a chairman who was responsible for searching the people for everything, including food items, oil, salt, firewood, rice, sauce, and vinegar. The people were exhausted all day long, unable to eat when hungry and unable to wear warm clothes when cold. If anyone spoke or expressed pain, they would be detained and punished. It was a great catastrophe for our family." (Guowen News Agency, December 10)

Shandong Province Grain Prices Plunge - Many Grain Merchants Experience Slow Business and Close Down ### 106

Jinan Dispatch: Recently, various industries in Shandong have been in a slump, almost reaching their lowest point. The drastic fall in grain prices is also unprecedented. For example, wheat, which was worth five or six yuan per hundred catties last year, is now only selling for three yuan. Sorghum, which was around four yuan last year, is now at two yuan and ten cents. Peanuts, which were seven yuan last year, are now at three yuan, fifty or sixty cents. Other grains have experienced similar declines. As a result, grain merchants in Jinan City are facing deserted storefronts with no business to be done. It is said that during the years of the Republic of China from 1927 to 1929, there were as many as 128 grain stores in Jinan City, marking a golden age. Afterwards, they gradually closed down, and this year, the number has decreased to around twenty. Many of them are also engaged in other businesses, such as coal stores, in order to survive. In reality, there are only a little more than ten left, including Tong Ju He, De Xing He, Heng Ju Cheng Yu Lai, Tong Ju Chang, Xie Tai Fu Xing Shun, and Fu Tong Ju Dong Xin Cheng Dong Fu Cheng Yong. It is said that the current situation is that while there are people selling grain, there are very few buyers. Although the price has been reduced, it still does not help the situation. The result of the grain price plunge is that cheap grain hurts farmers. Ignoring the surface, one might assume it is due to a good harvest in rural areas, overproduction, and supply exceeding demand; or that the transportation is not smooth and sales are stagnant. However, the actual situation now is the opposite. According to a survey by the Grain Industry Association, the agricultural production of various counties this year is not abundant and is only about 70% to 80% of a normal year, barely enough to sustain themselves. Furthermore, comparing the situation with previous years, before the three northeastern provinces were occupied by Japan, a large amount of sorghum was imported into Shandong from Qingdao and Yangjiaogou every year. In addition, Hebei in the north and Jiangsu in the south also gradually imported grain. At that time, not only did grain prices not fall, but there was no concern about unsalable goods. Now, since the loss of the three northeastern provinces, the steady stream of imports has disappeared. The actual amount of grain in the province has not only not increased compared to before, but has decreased, resulting in the current situation of cheap grain hurting farmers, which is quite strange. (16th)

Anhui Capital - Execution by Firing Squad of Manufacturer of "Red Pills" 107

Anqing Dispatch: The Anqing Military Police Joint Inspection Office received a tip-off on the 2nd of this month that Wu Xingfa, a resident of 52 Dong Street outside the Small South Gate of the provincial capital, was manufacturing "red pills" every night and transporting them to various towns and villages for sale. It was reported that ten pieces of goods had arrived from Shanghai a few days ago, and two pieces had already been sent across the river for transshipment one evening. The Inspection Director Dong Ziming and Inspector Bo Donghui were dispatched to the address with the local patrol officers to search the premises. They arrested the main offender Wu Xingfa, accomplices Ji Guoyuan, Wu He Shi, and Hu Xiaoyi, and seized several pieces of narcotics. The suspects and drugs were taken back to the office, and after interrogation by Director Li Yimin, the suspects confessed to manufacturing "red pills." Subsequently, the suspects were sent to the Anqing Garrison Headquarters, where, after clear interrogation, except for Wu He Shi and Hu Xiaoyi, whose involvement was considered minor and were sentenced to imprisonment and detention respectively and sent to prison for execution, and after notifying various agencies by letter and publicly burning the narcotics, the death penalty was imposed in accordance with the instructions of the Yuzhouwan Three-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters, attached to the Puyuanzi No. 51, and Article 57, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. After the approval of the provincial government, the main offenders Wu Xingfa and Ji Guoyuan were identified and taken to the execution ground outside the Small East Gate yesterday (the 13th) at 4:00 PM and executed by firing squad as a warning. Wu Xingfa was from Huaining, 42 years old, and Ji Guoyuan was from Shanghai, 28 years old. (December 14th)

Changshu - Meeting to Reduce Local Budget 110

The Jiangsu Provincial Government, to carefully reduce local surtaxes, has formed a review committee. The committee will thoroughly review the budgets submitted by various counties and order the county government to convene various agencies and local gentry to discuss budget reductions and surtax cuts. The county government held a meeting at the county government on the afternoon of the 18th of this month. After several hours of discussion, five important items were resolved. 1. The county's land tax surcharge is 4 jiao 7 fen 8 li per mu. Due to the sharp decline in production and low rice prices, this surcharge will be reduced by 1 jiao across the board. All surcharge names will be abolished, and the unified tax will be the county tax per mu. 2. The land survey fee is collected at 1 jiao per mu, with a term of three years. This year will be the last year. Currently, the people are suffering and cannot afford the burden. The land survey fee has been collected for two years, and a certain amount has been accumulated, enough to cover the start-up costs. The provincial department will be requested to postpone the collection for the time being until the land survey is actually carried out, and then it will be collected again. 3. Currently, rice prices have plummeted and land prices are falling. The highest land price is less than 50 yuan per mu, and no one is interested in buying it. However, the land price set by the County Land Bureau is 125 yuan per mu, which is too different from the market price. This has resulted in a distorted land tax structure, which has invisibly increased the burden on the people. The county should convene an assessment committee as soon as possible, and conduct a thorough investigation of the actual market price of the land and re-estimate it.

Zhang Wenxuan is the manager, and Ding Zufu is the assistant manager. The business is quite developed. However, at 2:40 AM yesterday (the 19th), a fire suddenly broke out. Zhenjiang - End of Shipping of Hunan's Huai Salt by Rotation 117

Xiang'an has always been a place for the sale of Huainan salt licenses, with a fixed quota of 120 tickets per year for rotation, so as to supplement the insufficiency of sail transport. Since the Yunshi Mu promoted rotation transport last year, the amount of rotation transport tickets at the port has been gradually increased year by year. It is estimated that 168 tickets should be handled this year, of which about 140 tickets are allocated to Jinan for sale and about 20 tickets are allocated to the three Huai Bei yards for sale. Although the salt from the three Huai Bei yards was transported in May and June, it was purely new production this year, with a higher moisture content, resulting in the discovery of thousands of bags of wet salt upon arrival. The port merchants secretly lamented their losses, and the users complained. The Jinan yard salt was shipped from August to the end of last month, and all of it has been shipped. It is reported that the inspection in Hunan showed that the color was white and clean, and the bags were dry, which was welcomed by the Hunan side.

Sun Ke Went to Hong Kong Last Night to Transfer to the Philippines - It is Said That This Trip Has Absolutely No Political Relationship - Scheduled to Return to Shanghai on the Original Ship on New Year's Day Next Year - He Will Visit Hu in Hong Kong in a Private Capacity 125

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, his wife, Yu Ming, the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yang Huari, the Secretary of the National Economic Council, and their sons, daughters, attendants, and servants, departed last night at 10:00 PM on the President Hoover of the Great Lai Company to Hong Kong and then to the Philippines. There is much speculation outside about Sun's sudden trip to the South, but last night, before his departure, Sun told the reporter of this newspaper that this trip had absolutely no political relationship. He will visit Hu Hanmin in Hong Kong in a private capacity to exchange views. He will stay in Manila for a short time and return on the original ship, hoping to return to Shanghai on New Year's Day next year. Details are recorded as follows:

Returned to Residence at Noon with Many Luggage 126

Liang Hancao, the Secretary-General of the Legislative Yuan, went to Sun's private residence on Columbia Road at around 9:00 AM yesterday to visit Sun and ask for instructions on everything. Sun then went out to visit friends and only returned to his residence at noon. In the afternoon, he packed his luggage and did not receive guests. The ship tickets were purchased by the China Travel Service. Sun himself bought a round-trip ticket between Shanghai and Manila. He brought a lot of luggage, including dozens of large and small boxes, which were fully loaded on a large truck of the China Travel Service at around 4:00 PM and transported to the ship in advance.

A Group of Eight Left Shanghai Last Night 127

Sun and his wife, along with Yu Ming, Yang Huari, their sons, daughters, attendants, and servants, a group of eight people, took a ferry from the New Customs Wharf at 8:45 PM last night to cross the river and board the President Hoover. The ship left Shanghai at 10:00 PM last night and is expected to arrive in Hong Kong on the afternoon of the 21st. The next day, the original ship will go to the Philippines. It is scheduled to rest in Manila for one or two days, and on the 27th, it will return to Shanghai on the President Hoover, hoping to return to Shanghai on New Year's Day next year.

Many People Went to New Customs Wharf to See Off 128

When Sun and his wife left Shanghai last night, those who went to the New Customs Wharf to see them off included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Liu Weizhi, the Vice Minister of Industry, Liang Hancao, the Secretary-General of the Legislative Yuan, Wu Jingxiong and Chen Jianru, members of the Legislative Yuan, Chen Qingyun, a member of the Central Committee, Li Zhaohuan, the President of Jiaotong University, Tang Shixuan, the Secretary of the Municipal Government, Li Dachao, the Chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government, and more than 20 relatives and friends of Sun. They left one after another after the ferry departed.

Sun Expressed a Private Trip 129

The reporter of this newspaper interviewed Sun on the ferry last night. According to him, this trip is purely a private trip and has absolutely no political relationship. My wife has recently been ill, and the doctor ordered her to breathe sea air, which is easier to recover her health. Therefore, I am taking a vacation for a sea trip. After I arrive in Manila, I will stay for a day or two and return to Shanghai on the original ship, hoping to return on New Year's Day next year. My wife may stay there longer. When passing through Hong Kong, the ship will stop for four or five hours, and I will visit Mr. Hu Zhantang in a private friendly capacity to exchange views. The trip to Guangzhou is not allowed due to time. I have telegraphed Chairman Chiang about my trip. The reporter then asked about Hu Hanmin's proposal to form another government. Sun did not express any opinion. When asked about various speculations about Sun's trip to the South, Sun repeatedly said that they were not accurate.

Yang Dezhao Also Returned South on the Same Ship 130

Yang Dezhao and his wife, Chen Jitang's representatives in Beijing and Shanghai, also left Shanghai on the same ship with Sun last night. After arriving in Hong Kong, Yang will go directly to Guangzhou to meet Chen and report everything. According to Yang, he told the reporter on the ship that this trip was entirely to celebrate his father's birthday and take care of personal matters, and there were no other tasks. It is not true that he reported on the matter of asking the central government to guarantee a loan. This loan does not require me to personally return to Guangdong to report. It will take about a month to return to Shanghai.

Military and Political Authorities Issue a Notice - Citizens Should Not Believe Rumors - Order Military and Police to Arrest Reactionary Elements 131

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, due to the spread of rumors by reactionary elements attempting to incite public sentiment, issued a notice jointly signed by the Municipal Government and the Songhu Garrison Command, which was issued to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and distributed to various districts for posting in the thoroughfares. The notice is recorded below: For the purpose of issuing a notice, since the suppression of bandits and communists in Jiangxi Province, there have been frequent reports of victory. The situation has progressed step by step, and the chaos will be quelled in the near future. Shanghai is the hub of Southeast China and has become an important town. At this time of national crisis, the security of the rear should be strengthened to ensure that the military in the front can achieve success as soon as possible. Recently, it has been found that unscrupulous people and reactionary elements are lurking in the urban area, spreading rumors, attempting to incite public sentiment, and conspiring to cause chaos. Their intentions are sinister and hateful. In addition to ordering the military and police to strictly investigate and arrest them for prosecution, all citizens must be secure in their occupations and must not lightly believe rumors and cause mutual panic. This notice is hereby issued for strict compliance.

Yuji Tilts - Passengers Rescued by Jiangyuan Warship 136

Yuda Company's Yuji ran aground on Donggua Island off the coast of Wenzhou. The first and second cabins were completely broken. Fortunately, the passengers on board were rescued by the naval vessel Jiangyuan and sent to Shanghai. It is heard that it can arrive in Shanghai that night. The Yuji has tilted to the surface of the sea, and the situation is very dangerous. Further news will be recorded as follows.

Ship Tilting and Frequent Danger 137

The location where the Yuji ran aground is near the Donggua Island Lighthouse off the coast of Wenzhou, about three hours by sea from Wenzhou. According to those familiar with the Shanghai-Fuzhou route, there are three routes through Zhejiang Ocean: outer, middle, and inner circles. Donggua Island is within the inner route circle, where there are many hidden reefs. According to people in the company, the Yuji's accident was probably caused by wind and waves, but the shipowner's telegram did not mention it. The company received a further telegram from the Yuji yesterday, stating that the first and second cabins were completely submerged, and the ship had become front-heavy and rear-light. In addition, due to the impact of the waves, the front of the ship was also grounded on the reef. From the afternoon of the 18th, the hull gradually tilted to one side, and the situation was very dangerous.

Jiangyuan Rescued Passengers 138

More than a hundred passengers gathered in the rear cabin after the accident to await rescue. Later, after receiving a telegram from Shanghai that Huadefeng Tugboat had been dispatched to rescue them, the passengers waited on the ship. The Jiangyuan and Chuguan warships sent by the Naval Department of Sandu came to the ship to protect them. However, by the afternoon, the hull of the Yuji gradually tilted, and the passengers on board were greatly panicked, fearing an accident. They asked the shipowner to consult with the Jiangyuan warship of the Navy to first transfer the passengers to the warship and send them to Shanghai. After the captain of the Jiangyuan warship agreed, they released a sampan for transfer and rescued all of them onto the warship that night.

Transported to Shanghai That Day 139

After the Jiangyuan warship rescued all the passengers, it sent a telegram to Shanghai, reporting to the Yuda Company that all the passengers had been rescued and were being transported to Shanghai by the ship. It is estimated that it will arrive in Shanghai on the night of the 19th. The shipowner also telegraphed to Shanghai, informing them that all the passengers had been safely rescued, with no casualties, and were being transported to Shanghai by Jiangyuan. The company, upon receiving this telegram, immediately consulted Huadefeng Tugboat, telling them that there was no need to sail for rescue.

Consultations on Rescue Measures 140

The person in charge of the Yuda Company said that the rescue plan for the Yuji is currently under negotiation. Yesterday, the company sent two telegrams to the Yuji shipowner, asking in detail about the extent of the damage to the ship and how to rescue it most effectively, whether to send a large ship to tow it, or to send a barge to unload the cargo first. After the reply, the method will be determined. The Lianbao Insurance Company, because it insured the ship for 120,000 yuan for peace insurance, advocated sending a ship to rescue the Yuji after it ran aground. It has contacted the company many times yesterday and has also decided to wait for the reply telegram to determine the rescue method, such as sending a ship to salvage it or sending personnel to inspect it.

Ship and Cargo Losses 141

The ship's hold cracked, the damage was enormous, and rescue was very difficult. The cargo inside the ship consisted entirely of oranges and olives, which were not affected by the water, but there were fears of decay over time and difficulties with unloading. The total value of the cargo was estimated to be over 100,000 yuan, and together with the "Yuji" ship itself, as well as the luggage of passengers and crew, the total loss was at least 300,000 yuan or more.

American Cotton and Wheat Arrive in Force - First Batch of Wheat Unloaded Yesterday - Four Ships to Arrive in Two Weeks - Totaling Over 32,000 Tons 142

American wheat arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and unloading began yesterday, which is expected to take four days to complete. The ship will then be returned to Baohe Company. The second batch, after arriving in Shanghai, is planned to load American goods for export. American cotton has also recently arrived in force, as detailed below.

First Batch Exclusively Purchased by Fufeng 143

The first shipment of American wheat, 8,940 tons transported by the "Arie Flaebank," was exclusively purchased by the Fufeng Flour Mill in Shanghai. The Fuxin Mill did not receive any. Therefore, after the ship arrived in Shanghai and underwent routine inspection, unloading began yesterday morning. Fufeng sent barges to Wharf No. 4 to receive the cargo, which was then barged to Suzhou Creek and stored in the mill's own warehouses, exempt from import duties. This has been approved by the Ministry of Finance, making the purchase of American wheat even cheaper than ordering directly from the United States. After this batch of cargo is unloaded, the ship will be returned to Baohe, as it needs to be sent to Little Luzon to transport goods to Mumbai, India. Therefore, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will not continue to lease this ship.

Next Shipment to Carry Goods for Export 144

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has secured over 5,000 tons of American goods for export. However, since the first ship was scheduled to return immediately after arriving in Shanghai, the large shipment of goods destined for the United States will be transported on the second ship carrying wheat to Shanghai. The second batch of wheat, 8,000 tons, is expected to arrive within this week, and two more batches, totaling 12,700 tons, are expected to arrive in another ten days. In total, 32,213 tons can be transported within these two weeks, worth approximately 2.3 million yuan in national currency.

Ships Transport Cotton One After Another 145

Imports of American cotton have also recently arrived in large quantities. In addition to the 5,500 bales transported by the Yitai Foreign Firm's "Chevrolet" ship, other British and American ships have transported varying amounts of one to two thousand bales each. The Fulai Foreign Firm has also loaded two ships, including the "Delating," each carrying four to five thousand bales. These are being unloaded at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's North Wharf and China Wharf. An additional 10,000 bales of American cotton destined for Shanghai in January are currently en route.

Various Places Inquire About Purchasing American Wheat 146

Flour mills in various locations have recently heard that importing American wheat with loans is exempt from tariffs, and the cost is lower than buying directly from abroad. Therefore, in recent days, Tianjin, Hankou, Ningbo, and other places have been inquiring about wheat prices and negotiating purchase matters with the American Wheat Management Office. From next month onwards, shipments to China will increase, with at least 40,000 tons imported each month.

Ministry of Finance Revises Regulations on Native Tobacco Leaves - Refund of Special Tax Method - Instructs Tax Bureaus and Revenue Agencies - All Tax Refund Requests Must Be Verified with Evidence 147

Regarding native tobacco leaves that have already paid the special tax and are transported for sale abroad and in non-special tax areas, merchants should, according to regulations, submit all required evidence to the original special tax collection agency to request a tax refund. The Ministry of Finance has revised and supplemented the tax refund method and has specifically instructed the Tax Bureau and all native tobacco tax bureaus to comply. The original text is transcribed below:

Special Tax Paid 148

For native tobacco leaves exported from Shanghai to foreign countries and non-special tax areas, merchants should be allowed to collect all necessary evidence after reporting the export and submit it to the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau for verification and tax refund. For those reporting transportation to other ports or foreign and non-special tax areas, merchants should be allowed to submit evidence directly to the agency that originally approved the transportation for export to request a tax refund. Those holding original tax payment certificates at the border of a special tax area and reporting transportation for sale in a non-special tax area should still request a tax refund directly from the original special tax collection agency. When the Tax Bureau encounters merchants submitting Shanghai export evidence to request a tax refund, if the evidence is verified to be true,

Tax Refund Should Be Granted 149

The tax bureau should calculate the amount of tax to be refunded according to regulations, fill out a tax refund certificate, and have the merchant find a shop guarantor. The tax bureau will then issue the refund in full and send the original evidence and tax refund certificate to the provincial bureau or special tobacco tax office that originally collected the special tax, as well as the consolidated tax management office that also handles tobacco taxes, instructing them to return the amount of the advance tax refund to the Tax Bureau for reimbursement. After receiving the merchant's receipt and tax refund certificate issued by the Tax Bureau, the provincial bureau, special tobacco tax office, and consolidated tax management office that also handle tobacco taxes should then submit a request to the Tax Bureau to offset the tax amount in accordance with the tax offset method listed in Article 3. When provincial stamp tax bureaus for tobacco and alcohol, special tobacco tax offices, and consolidated tax management offices that also handle tobacco taxes encounter merchants submitting evidence when reporting the direct transportation or transportation of native tobacco leaves to foreign countries and non-special tax areas

Submit Evidence 150

When requesting a tax refund, if the evidence is verified to be true and a tax refund should be granted, the amount of tax to be refunded should be calculated according to regulations, a tax refund certificate should be filled out, and the merchant should provide a shop guarantee. The refund should be issued in full from the collected tax funds. After obtaining the merchant's receipt, a tax offset form should be filled out, and the original receipt and tax refund certificate should be submitted to the Tax Bureau to offset the tax amount. When tobacco and alcohol tax sub-bureaus and special tobacco tax sub-bureaus encounter merchants submitting evidence when reporting the direct transportation of native tobacco leaves to non-special tax areas and requesting a tax refund, they should immediately verify that the documents match and then submit the original documents to the provincial stamp tax bureau for tobacco and alcohol or the special tobacco tax office, and the consolidated tax management office that also handles tobacco taxes for review. A tax refund certificate should be filled out according to regulations and issued to the merchant through the sub-bureau.

Find a Shop Guarantee 151

The refund should be issued in full from the collected tax funds. The original documents should be canceled and retained by the provincial bureau or special tobacco tax office, and the consolidated tax management office that also handles tobacco taxes. After obtaining the merchant's receipt, a tax offset form should be filled out, and the original receipt and tax refund certificate should be submitted to the provincial bureau or special tobacco tax office, and the consolidated tax management office that also handles tobacco taxes that originally issued the tax refund certificate to offset the tax amount. After receiving the merchant's receipt and tax refund certificate submitted by the sub-bureau, the provincial bureau or special tobacco tax office, and the consolidated tax management office that also handles tobacco taxes should then submit a request to the Tax Bureau to offset the tax amount in accordance with the tax offset method listed in Article 3 above.

Whereabouts of Contemporary Figures 152

Liang Hanchao and Chen Qingyun took the night express train to Beijing last night. Xu Shiying took the night express train out of Beijing last night and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

At the same time, the design drawings for the two major buildings, the library and the museum, in the central area have been drafted and are scheduled to be completed within two years. The details are divided as follows:

Relocation Dates of Municipal Government Bureaus 155

After the Municipal Government meeting decided that the period from the 15th to the 31st of this month would be the relocation date for the Municipal Government and various bureaus, each bureau immediately actively prepared everything. After deliberation, the deadline for the relocation of each bureau was decided as follows: 1. Social Affairs Bureau on the 20th, 2. Secretariat on the 25th, 3. Health Bureau on the 25th, 4. Education Bureau on the 26th, 5. Public Works Bureau on the 26th, 6. Land Bureau on the 24th, 7. Finance and Public Utilities Bureaus to postpone relocation. Representatives of Qinlian Sugar Merchants Asked the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for Assistance Yesterday 157

The export of native sugar from Qinlian, Guangdong, to Shanghai has been repeatedly identified by the Jianghai Customs as being mixed with foreign sugar, and huge fines have been imposed. Sugar merchants have repeatedly suffered losses, and all have suspended business and transportation. The farmers in more than ten counties in southern Guangdong, who rely on the sugar industry for their livelihood, are also on the verge of unemployment and bankruptcy due to the severance of sales channels. All sectors of Qinlian believe that it is urgently necessary to find a way to maintain it. Therefore, the Beihai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, together with the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce and the Qinlian Sugar Industry Guangyi Hall, sent representative Pang Songhui to the province and Beijing to petition. The situation has been reported in previous newspapers. The representative arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday. The Cantonese sugar merchants in Shanghai, Guang'an Hall, specially held a banquet for Representative Pang at the New Asia Hotel to report the facts of the case and the situation of petitioning in the province, and the two sides discussed relief methods and steps. At 1:00 p.m. yesterday, accompanied by sugar merchant Ye Boming and others, Representative Pang went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to request assistance. Zhang Bofang, director of the business department of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, received him. Representative Pang talked about the detailed process and the four methods of petitioning in this case, and handed over the joint letter from the Qinlian Chambers of Commerce. Mr. Zhang said that the Chamber has repeatedly telegraphed the central ministries and departments to fight for the case of Jianghai Customs fining native sugar. Now it will forward the four items mentioned in the letter to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry for a fair solution as soon as possible. The public letter from the Qinlian Chambers of Commerce to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce is copied as follows: With respect, according to the letter from Qinlian Sugar Industry Guangyi Hall, "We have received a letter from our colleagues Heli, Henghe Long, Guangchang, and Heyi, stating that from July to September of this year, our colleagues shipped native white sugar from Beihai to Shanghai five times. All of them were inspected by the Beihai Customs and confirmed to be pure native sugar, and the transit tax was paid in accordance with the regulations before being released. Unexpectedly, the original shipment was directly transported to Shanghai and was completely detained by the Jianghai Customs Tax Department, claiming that it was mixed with 10% to 20% foreign sugar. A total of 1,560 yuan of ocean money was fined and 1,957 yuan of tax was supplemented. The method used to distinguish native sugar from foreign sugar is without standards and has many errors. Our colleagues have jointly submitted a telegram to argue the case, but it has not been resolved for more than a month. Our colleagues are innocent and have suffered this major loss, forcing them to temporarily suspend business to await relief. We have specially listed the list of fines for each company and ask you to check it and immediately forward it to the Beihai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Qinlian County Chambers of Commerce, and report it to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, ordering the Jianghai Customs Tax Department to return the fines in full to show fairness," etc. Beihai is an important port for the export of native sugar in South China. The Beihai Customs is close to the sugar-producing area and has a clear understanding of the composition of native sugar and the difference between it and foreign sugar. Therefore, our colleagues have always reported the native sugar for inspection and release, and there has never been a misunderstanding or difficulty. Now that the original shipment is directly transported to Shanghai, the Jianghai Customs claims that it is mixed with foreign sugar and imposes huge fines, which is obviously abusing its powers to destroy local products. If it is not stopped according to the law, how can farmers and merchants live in peace? We have specially recorded the letter and ask you to forward the report to relieve the suffering of merchants, etc., as approved by the Chamber of Commerce. Since the Jianghai Customs' deduction of native sugar occurred, sugar merchants have stopped transporting, and the losses have been unbearable. The farmers and workers in more than ten counties who rely on the sugar industry for their livelihood are also at risk of unemployment and bankruptcy. Livelihood and security are greatly affected. According to the letter, we should deal with the livelihood of farmers and merchants in more than ten counties. Therefore, we have specially joined the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce to convene public associations such as the sugar industry and all sugar merchants to discuss relief methods. A total of four items were agreed upon: 1. Please ask the Ministry of Finance to correct the Jianghai Customs' erroneous method of inspecting the difference between native sugar and foreign sugar. 2. Please ask the Ministry of Finance to order the Jianghai Customs to release the native sugar of Beihai sugar merchants and return the past fines and supplementary taxes. 3. Please ask the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Finance to instruct all customs offices across the country to protect the safety of native sugar imports and exports and not to deliberately make things difficult. 4. Please ask the Central Government to issue an order to exempt native sugar from export and transit taxes and set up export incentives for native sugar. After unanimous adoption, in addition to telegrams and submissions, we have specially recorded the case and handed it to your association, and sent Representative Pang Songhui to present everything in person, please give practical assistance so that this case can be thoroughly resolved as soon as possible. It is not only the luck of the Qinlian sugar industry, but also the luck of the national business."

Our overseas Chinese compatriots in Mexico have been oppressed by the anti-Chinese party in Mexico. There have been 19 batches of returnees one after another. Ministry of Finance Instructs Silver Money Industry to Submit Precious Silver - Deadline of One Month to Hand Over Stocked Precious Silver - Lin Kanghou Talks About the Complete Abolition of Taels in Half a Year 159

According to Shenshi News Agency in this city, the Ministry of Finance decided to abolish taels for yuan in order to thoroughly reform the currency system, stipulating that 7 qian 1 fen 5 li is a fixed conversion rate, which has been implemented since March 10. The Ministry issued a clear order to the two Silver Money Guilds to implement it together, and then prohibited the melting and casting of silver furnaces as a fundamental abolition plan. However, the silver tael system has a long history and is deeply rooted. Once abolished, it will not be easy. The Ministry of Finance yesterday instructed the two Silver Money Guilds to hand over the stocked precious silver within a time limit, which is the final method to fundamentally abolish silver taels. The details are recorded in detail as follows:

Ministry of Finance Orders to Hand Over Precious Silver 160

The Ministry of Finance believes that the power of the two Silver Money Guilds in this city has always been strong. Although it has repeatedly issued clear orders to abolish taels, the fundamental reason why all parties still follow the old system and have not completely abolished it is that the existing silver in stock has not been changed, which is a major obstacle to currency system reform. Now the Ministry of Finance has specially instructed the two Silver Money Guilds to hand over all stocked precious silver to the Central Bank within one month and exchange it for silver dollars in accordance with the stipulated conversion rate. After the deadline, precious silver must no longer be used as a reserve. The Central Mint has separately minted a kind of thousand-yuan silver bar, with one thousand silver dollars per bar, which can be used as a reserve for various banks or money shops, which is very convenient.

Effect of Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan 161

Yesterday, a reporter from Shenshi News Agency interviewed Mr. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the Banking Association, and asked about the effect of the Ministry of Finance's order to abolish taels and change to yuan. According to him, the market has been reformed a lot since the Ministry of Finance ordered the abolition of taels and the change to yuan, and silver taels will no longer be used. Recently, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Silver Money Industry to hand over precious silver within one month and exchange it for silver coins. After that, the inventory is empty and there is no basis, so silver taels will no longer be issued in the market. However, due to various habitual relationships, it may not be completely eliminated temporarily. According to my observation, the goal of completely abolishing taels can definitely be achieved in another six months.

The Case of Jin Xi's Arrest - The French Consul Has Notified the Japanese Consul of Release - But Has Not Received a Reply, So He Has Not Notified Jin's Family 165

It has been nearly a month since Jin Xi was illegally arrested by the French Concession Central Patrol Room in cooperation with the Japanese Consulate General in the French Concession. The family members have presented the Chinese citizenship permit of Jin Yongduo and Jin Xi through representatives Li Shichang and lawyer Xu Jie, and have inquired with the French Concession Central Patrol Room one after another. On the 6th of this month, lawyer Xu Jie and Li Shichang negotiated with the French Consul General's Office, and the French Consul General agreed to notify the Japanese Consul General's Office to send back Jin Xi. Lawyers Xu Jie and Lou Yunmei formally represented the case in writing, requesting the French Consul General's Office to notify the Japanese Consul General's Office to send back the case. The afternoon before yesterday, lawyer Xu Jie visited the French Consul General's Office again and had a long conversation with the French Consul General. According to the French Consul General, the French Consulate General had formally notified the Japanese Consul General in writing a long time ago, but has not yet replied. He will notify Jin Xi's family as soon as he receives a reply.

A special regulation was issued before the test, stipulating that they must report within six months to wait for the test. Unexpectedly, the foreign crew members ignored the Ministry's order and did not take the test. After the deadline, they still worked on the ship. The Shanghai Merchant Ship Driving Association and the Marine Engineering Association submitted a request to the Ministry, requesting the implementation of the crackdown, replacing all these unauthorized foreign crew members and suspending their duties. The Ministry has approved the order and ordered the Shanghai Maritime Administration to strictly implement it. The Maritime Administration has begun to inspect the employment of foreign crew members on national ships entering and leaving the country in compliance with the Ministry's order. If anyone is found without a certificate, the departure form will not be issued and the ship will be prohibited from leaving the country. This time, the captain and mate of the Yu Da ship were foreign nationals and had no certificates. Therefore, the crackdown was implemented, and the ship was prohibited from leaving the country, causing Yu Da to be stranded in Shanghai for two days. As a result, the ship asked a Chinese second mate to come forward and take the place, and submitted an application in accordance with the regulations. The company promised to replace the unauthorized crew members and replace them with qualified personnel before being allowed to leave the country. Recently, the Maritime Administration has been very serious about handling this matter. After this rectification, foreign crew members must be examined and approved by the Ministry's order.

The Ship Collision Committee Held Its Sixth Meeting Yesterday and Resolved Methods for Handling the Fuxing Wheel Dispute, etc. 175

The Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Communications held its sixth committee meeting at the bureau at nine o'clock yesterday morning. The attendees were Zhu Yaoting (represented by Yu Shifan), Yu Shifan, Sha Huijia, Xu Zufan, and Zhang Zhuzun. Zou Zhidong attended as an observer. The chairman was Zhu Yaoting (represented by Yu Shifan), and the recorder was Zhu Guanying. After the usual formalities, the chairman reported the details of the ship collisions in each case. Then, the discussion began. Proposal 1: To determine the amount of compensation that the Dahua ship of the Pingan Shipping Company should pay to the Daxing ship for damage repair costs. Resolution: Calculate the repair costs based on a 60% discount on the repair bill submitted by the Fuxing wheel. The lost income during the downtime should be included in full. Both should be paid by the Dahua wheel. Proposal 2: The Baohua wheel of the Pingan Shipping Company and the Daxing No. 1 wheel of the Daxing Shipping Company collided near the Taiping Port in Beisha. Resolution: The Daxing No. 1 wheel should be responsible for 70% of the negligence, and the Baohua wheel should be responsible for 30% of the negligence. The meeting adjourned at one o'clock and fifteen minutes.

More Than 1,000 Japanese Navy Personnel Land in Song for Sightseeing, Landing Yesterday Morning and Returning to Their Ships in the Afternoon 176

At around nine o'clock yesterday morning, more than a thousand Japanese Navy personnel successively landed at the Liangmi Stack Wharf in Zhanghuabang, Wusong. All of them were unarmed. They then toured the outer road of Wusong Town and went to the Huafeng Spinning Factory, a Japanese-owned factory on Yunzao Road. At that time, residents were surprised by the sudden arrival of a large number of Japanese soldiers. Later, reporters inquired with the public security authorities, who said that they had been notified by their superiors that two Japanese training ships would arrive in Song that day, but due to tidal conditions, they could not enter the port. The navy landed nearby for sightseeing and had no other intentions. Therefore, the police, led by District Chief Xi of the Seventh Public Security District and Yao, the head of the first branch of the Seventh Public Security District, and Officer Li of the water patrol team, were dispatched to take care of the situation. At that time, the Wusong Chamber of Commerce also notified all shops in the town not to misunderstand.
